if (is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png') && (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png') != '11d1d079f8cb6457448334c2098c1f904c07db9d')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png') != '11d1d079f8cb6457448334c2098c1f904c07db9d') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/fourcc/img/general_leaf_icon16.png');
}
